name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:View Tiger Deluxe Queenroom

info:1 Review
rating:4
posted:Posted March 18, 2024
msg:Overall feeling:
Except for the positive reviews about the room, everything else was average. The room booked as a surprise came with a blind box (a tiger doll backpack, which children love).
stay:
The room is big enough, clean, and has no smell, but there is a smell outside the corridor of the room (note that).
Peripheral facilities:
It is small, with only a zoo and a swimming pool (inside the water park outside), and the water park will not be open to the public until May 1. For other entertainment, you need to go to Pingnan Square by taxi or Didi.
food:
Breakfast (the breakfast buffet included in the hotel package, the food has a lot of variety for breakfast, and the taste is normal), lunch is at your own expense (price comparison is average, the pictures have receipts and dishes), and I chose the hotel buffet for dinner (the food variety is small, and the dishes are not enough) ''Guests'' are quick, the portions are small, and filling is slow. They have to grab to get something to eat. I'm really speechless)
Hotel reception staff: good service attitude and patient answers
Restaurant staff: In addition to constantly reminding guests to leave comments, the service attitude is as good as the hotel reception.
suggestion:
In addition to the food at the buffet night, the daily tiger teasing time can be extended a little longer. Some toys or small climbing frames suitable for the tigers should be added outside the window of the tiger viewing room to guide the tigers to also play with the tigers during the feeding time. Go to the room to watch the guests, because the tigers will not go to the tiger viewing room on their own, and the guests do not have to interact with the tigers. In fact, they donâ€™t need to stay in such a high-end room, but can stay in an ordinary room (the room size is the same but the price Qualified differences).
The zoo should add more manpower to reduce the serious disrepair caused by the shortage of manpower and the lack of manpower to manage the hygienic environment and physical condition of the animals. It is hoped that the zoo can slowly add manpower to improve the overall environment and hygiene inside and outside the park. In this way In order to attract more guests to come and play.

msg:When checking in at the hotel lobby, you can see tigers when you look up, but it is only available during the day, and there seems to be a time limit, because tigers are not there all day. We booked a twin room, the room is large, the bathroom is also large, the whole room is clean, tidy and beautiful.
This room type comes with 2 tickets to the Pingnan Xiongsen Animal World Scenic Area, a single ticket to the double water park and a single ticket to the double cute pet park, but the water park is not open in winter, and the cute pet park is not open at present. This room type includes breakfast, which has a lot of variety, but there are also many tourists. You can see tigers in the restaurant, and children will be very happy. Next, let me talk about what I am very dissatisfied with. First, for all tickets and meals, as long as the child is over one meter, you need to buy a child ticket, which is rare in major scenic spots and hotels. Usually, children over 1.2 meters are charged, but here they are charged for over one meter. Second, the biggest feature of Xiongsen Animal World is that there are many tigers, but the scenic map shows that there are pelicans, turtles, etc., and we didn't see them. If there are none, don't show them.
